;
; Well, that's the end of the list.
;
; I have deliberately omitted vendor ID FFFF which is actually "Undefined"
; deliberately by the PCI SIG. Software looks for FFFF to know if it's found a
; device or not; a vendor ID <>FFFF means you found a device, FFFF means no
; device present.
;
; The theory is that software would never look in the list for a possible
; vendor ID match when it's already knowing that there is no device there to
; get a match with! In the interest of human readability, therefore, this note
; is here and I hope it helped you!
;
